name:C‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äçl‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äç ‚ÄçJ‚Äço‚Äçy
info:Deluxe City View King
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Couples
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted March 22, 2024
msg:Stayed here for a couples Valentine's getaway. The staff were amazing, truly attentive and professional! The staff at both the main desk and in the restaurant were exemplary. We booked a package that included an afternoon tea, a dining voucher and breakfast. The afternoon tea was delightful and presented very well, the dinner was of average quality but the staff made the visit worthwhile. Breakfast featured a wide range of both Western and Chinese choices, so there was something for everyone. 
Our main reason for staying was to access the spa facilities, but we were disappointed that the jacuzzis in both the male and female changing areas were not working, and were rebranded as 'cold pools' which was very unfortunate- there was no all-gender jacuzzi as far as we could tell, which was also disappointing in itself. The sauna rooms in both changing areas were turned off, and we had to ask a member of staff to turn on the heat for us. Since the hotel is spa/wellness based, the only option being a standard swimming pool was a huge downside! We had booked this hotel for the spa facilities, and wouldn't recommend this to anyone looking for good facilities unless you are maybe looking to book one of the expensive massage packages. The hotel itself is lovely with well maintained rooms and fantastic staff, but the spa element was a letdown.
----------------------------------------

msg:Xiaya Hotel is located next to the Hu-Qingping Highway in Qingpu District, close to the town of Xiadu. We stayed here for several days during the epidemic last year and felt very good, but we always forgot to write a review. During the National Day this year, we came to Xiaya again. The English name of Xiadu Town is lidoway. After searching online for a long time, I still don‚Äôt know the origin of this name. I happened to drive by the Shanghaojia Factory on the nearby Shanghai-Qingping Highway in the past two days and found out that the English name of Shanghaojia Factory is Liwayway (Shanghaojia is a Philippine company), maybe the two have some connection, btw: Char minibar has a lot of Liwayway snacks, haha.

Serve:
On the first day of check-in, the hotel sent welcome fruits, desserts and sparkling wine, which was very thoughtful. Manager Necia is very nice and approachable, and her service is very attentive. She enthusiastically helped solve various problems, big and small. I was very touched! Every employee you meet in the hotel will greet you warmly and proactively, and is very professional. I believe that Xiaya will get better and better with employees like you.

health:
The hotel's hygiene is very good, and the bathrooms are equipped with smart sanitary ware as standard.

Location transportation:
The hotel is located in Qingpu District, Shanghai, at the entrance of Xiadu Town, a 10-minute drive from Panlong Tiandi. It is half an hour's drive from Xiayang Lake in Qingpu City, Sheshan Mountain in Songjiang District, Happy Valley, Guangfulin, and Chenshan Botanical Garden. One kilometer away is the entrance to the G15 Shenhai Expressway. You can get to Zhujiajiao in half an hour on the expressway, where the scenery of Dadian Lake is beautiful.

parking:
Parking at the hotel is very convenient. The entrance to the Xiaya underground parking lot is close to the entrance to the Xiadu Town Pedestrian Street. You need to call the front desk to report every time you drive out, and it will be valid within 15 minutes.

Room facilities:
The hotel opened in 2017 and the facilities are well maintained. The room has wooden floors. That is, there is no hard separation between the bathroom and the room, but a liftable curtain. When the bathroom is opened and closed, the curtain will make a sound. L'Occitane toiletries are also used in the ordinary rooms. The suite uses Italian Acqua di Parma water, which is very good. In addition, the room furniture has limitations on the size of the TV due to its original design. The balcony of the suite feels very nice. The weather is not hot recently. It is very comfortable to sit on the balcony and look into the distance with a cup of coffee.

Spa: The full name of the hotel is "The Senz Hotel & Spa", so the hotel's spa is also a special feature. I tried the 598 package this time and I was very satisfied!

breakfast:
Breakfast is on the first floor. The hotel's breakfast is quite good. Although there is not a lot of variety, it is very exquisite. There are Chinese and Western food, such as small steamed buns, siomai, wontons, chicken wings, etc., which all taste good, and there are also various fruits. The latest opening hours are 6:30-10:00 in the morning

swimming pool:
The swimming pool is on the underground floor, very clean, 20*10 meters, water depth 1.2-1.4 meters, very good swimming pool. The latest opening hours are 7:00 am-21:00 pm

Senz Charia Hotel is a very suitable hotel for weekend getaways and business trips. I will definitely come back next time!

The first time I stayed in the elegant garden view room in Char, the second time I came to participate in the Oktoberfest, I upgraded the executive garden view room, the scenery is similar, the room has a capsule coffee machine and 4 coffee capsules, the rest of the mini bar, L'Occitane set The same one. The feeling is quite high-grade. It would be better if the TV in the room can be changed to a larger size.
The cafe in the hotel is very sensual. There are outdoor garden seats. Both times, I sat in the garden for an afternoon, and had a deluxe version of afternoon tea and a cup of latte and cold beer. It was very comfortable. . . . Breakfast is also eaten in a cafe, and the meals are a bit German-style.
In the cafe, I can always see a foreigner serving, mostly helping to pour the coffee. On the last day, I learned that he is the general manager, disrespectful. The managers of the cafe are very enthusiastic, focusing on praising Leo, hoping that the business will be booming.
The hotel's swimming pool is good, 1.2 meters deep, with three lanes. There are not so many coaches with students, so it is very comfortable and clean. The only downside is that the lounge chairs next to it are all sponge sofa beds. If there is a wet person sitting on it the day before, it will not dry out for a few days, and it will be a lot of water.
The front desk service, except for a girl wearing glasses, has a somewhat xxxxx attitude, all the others are very good and feel at home. Thanks for all their help.
Finally, the hotel's exclusive parking space is a bit small. There are so many people coming to the Oktoberfest. We stayed there for three days. We didn't dare to drive the car when we stopped, because we were afraid that there would be nowhere to put it back.
In addition, if the car is parked in the underground parking space, you must remember to report to the front desk, otherwise you will have to pay to go out. Although the hotel said that it is possible to withdraw, it still feels very troublesome.
